Statement from the Chinese Seamen's Organizations Federation 154

The Chinese Seamen's Organizations Federation sent a letter to this newspaper stating, "To the editor: We were surprised to read a report in a certain newspaper about the KMT Party Headquarters banning our organization. Upon investigation, this federation is a formal organization composed of the China Marine Engineers United General Association, the China Merchant Ship Captains General Association, the China Merchants Bureau Jun'an Association, the China Ship Wireless Operators Public Welfare Association, the Nautical Magazine, the Northern Jun'an Public Association, the Jardine Matheson Wharf Workers Club, the Yan Ying General Association, and other formal organizations. It is entirely driven by patriotic enthusiasm, with pure motives and a clear stance, without the slightest political agenda. After its establishment, the KMT Maritime Affairs Party Affairs Representative, Comrade Wang Zhonggang, visited the federation to inspect its meeting minutes, simple summaries, and declarations. Furthermore, a Yang special representative was dispatched and scheduled to convene a meeting with responsible individuals from all parties on the 14th (today). We have also submitted a request for record-keeping to various KMT party and government agencies in this city. Therefore, the news of banning our organization is clearly a fabrication and malicious slander. We have always admired your newspaper's fair reporting and believe that it will show sympathy for patriotic movements. We are sending this special letter to state the facts and hope that you will publish the original letter to the highest degree of public knowledge. Yours sincerely, etc."

Theft Case at Minhua Primary School: Incomplete and Untrue Inside Story; Female Teacher's Waistcoat and Shorts Brought to Court as Evidence; Dispute over Rights and Jealousy Leading to This Situation 161

Yu Shangxun, the principal of Minhua Primary School, a Ningbo native, located at No. 10, Lane 251, Weihaiwei Road, had a Western suit and other items worth 77 yuan stolen on October 5th of last year. Recently, teacher Ding Jiasheng (also known as Ding Hao), a local native, was discovered to be a prime suspect. Therefore, on the 4th of the month, he reported to the Chengdu Road Police Station, instructing Detective Yang Xinzheng to arrest Ding. In Ding's suitcase, four pawn tickets were found, two of which belonged to a portion of the stolen items from Yu. He was then prosecuted in the First Special Court under Article 320 of the Criminal Law. Because the defendant claimed that the cause of this case was due to a love affair, specifically because the defendant's lover, Shen Shuqing (also a teacher at the school), had shifted her affections to Principal Yu, he was framed and slandered. The court considered it necessary to summon Shen Shuqing from Foshan, so it ordered a postponement. Ding Jiasheng was allowed to be released on bail of 100 yuan. Yesterday morning was the date for the continued hearing of this case. Many men and women from the education community attended the court to listen. First, Officer Jiang Baolian of the police station stated that the subpoena for Shen Shuqing had been delivered by the police and received by Yu Shangxun. Today, Shen has complied with the summons and arrived in court, requesting the court to question her. Yang Guanchang took the initiative to instruct Yu Shangxun to the case, telling him that if the defendant had committed theft, why would he hide the pawn tickets in his suitcase as evidence for the future? Wouldn't he be more likely to make it known and deliberately publicize that there were pawn tickets worth five or sixty yuan so that people would report him? However, Yu firmly insisted that it was Ding Jiasheng who had stolen the items without a doubt. The fact that the pawn tickets were found in his suitcase and that he had asked someone to mediate afterwards all proved it. The court then instructed Shen Shuqing to come to court. According to her statement, she had been acting on behalf of Principal Yu since October 1st of last year because he was suffering from a foot ailment, until the 10th of that month. On the morning of the 6th of this month, she went to the school to work and saw that the lock on the principal's office door had been broken. She entered the room and saw that the clothes hanging on the clothes rack and placed in the cabinet had disappeared. Knowing that there had been a theft, she reported it to the police station and asked Yu Shangxun about the number of stolen clothes, made a list, and submitted it to the police station. Police lawyer Jiang immediately asked if there were any of her clothes or belongings in the defendant's suitcase. She replied, "Not a single item." He asked, "Do you live in the same room with the defendant?" She replied, "No." Then, witness Zhu Bin, a teacher at the school, submitted a case, proving that Shen had planted the pawn tickets in the defendant's suitcase on the 2nd of the month (as reported in the previous newspaper). He also stated that Principal Yu was afraid that I would come to court to testify on the 6th, so he left a letter for me on the 5th, instructing me not to change the exam subjects for the 6th, intending to control me, while other teachers in the school did not receive such letters. He then submitted the letter to the court. The court asked Zhu whether the principal was at school on the evening of October 5th. He replied, "Not at school, he stayed in a small house." Shen Shuqing completely denied the points of framing made by Zhu Bin, stating that she had filed a separate lawsuit against Zhu and others. When questioned, Ding Jiasheng stated that this case was completely due to a love triangle and jealousy. Shen's statement that there was nothing of hers in his suitcase was not true. Her close-fitting waistcoat, shorts, qipao, etc., were all in his suitcase and had been brought to court today. Because of the plaintiffs' framing and slander, he had suffered significant damage to his spirit and reputation. Therefore, he was filing a counterclaim, requesting that the plaintiff be punished with the crime of false accusation under Article 169, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, and be ordered to issue a statement in the newspaper and compensate him for one yuan in damages. He then presented the underwear and other items to the court. However, Shen denied that the clothing belonged to her. The court then instructed Shen to wear one of the qipaos and then announced the start of the debate. Lawyer Sun Shi'an, representing the initial plaintiff, argued that this case was actually caused by a struggle for rights and jealousy. Therefore, he requested that the defendant be declared innocent. Finally, Ding also claimed that he knew Shen's hidden marks on her body well. The court, having understood, announced the end of the debate and set the date for sentencing this week. The defendant's counterclaim should be filed separately.

China Youth Basketball Tournament Opens 165

Thirty-Seven Teams Compete Every Tuesday and Thursday; Four Group Championships Set Up for Schools, Banks, Businesses, and Women

The 7th China Youth Men's and Women's Basketball League is scheduled to begin competing at the China Youth Sports Hall at 5:00 PM today. The pre-registration was exceptionally enthusiastic, with a total of thirty-seven teams participating. Four group championships have been set up for schools, banks, businesses, and women. Each Tuesday and Thursday, one match will be played. Each time there are five matches. Once the association's volleyball league concludes, Saturday will be added for a final decision, with three matches required each week. The competition will use a single round-robin system, and the rules will follow the basketball rules of 1935-36 announced by the Physical Education Association. Because there are nineteen participants in the business group, they are divided into three sections for competition. There are only four teams in the women's group, so it is scheduled to begin early next month. The league was originally scheduled to open before Christmas last winter, but due to insufficient preparation, it was postponed to today. Last year, only three groups were set up for schools, banks, and women. The championship in the school group was won by the YMCA High School, the bank group by the Shanghai Bank, and the women's group by the Black Hawk team. The business group is a newly added one this year. In addition to the exceptionally complicated participants in the previous season, the spirit was inevitably distracted. Therefore, this year, the recruitment was changed to an invitation to improve performance. There will be five games played today, one each in the school, bank, and business groups 1, 2, and 3. In addition, due to the small size of the sports hall, those who wish to visit will be charged a small entrance fee of one corner to show restrictions. The order for today is recorded as follows.

Education News

The Municipal Education Bureau's Alternative Make-Up Examination Methods After the Postponement of This Year's Joint Entrance Examination; Make-Up Examinees in This City Will Participate in Their Original School's Graduation Exam; Make-Up Examinations for Entrusted Examinees Will Be Held After the Start of the Semester 175

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "It has been decided that the graduation joint entrance examination for students in middle schools, normal schools, and physical education normal schools in this city this semester will be postponed after being approved by the Ministry of Education. Graduating classes of each school should hold graduation exams. All students who failed three subjects in previous joint entrance examinations and students who were entrusted by various provinces and cities to take the exam should wait for the make-up exam of the joint entrance examination in the next semester. This has been announced and made known to everyone. However, according to the students in this city and various provinces and cities who should participate in this year's joint entrance examination make-up exam, the time for the joint entrance examination in the next semester is still a long way off, and they have requested that alternative make-up examinations be held to facilitate further education. In order to take care of the studies of the make-up exam students in each school and quickly complete the joint entrance examination procedures for each student, the Bureau has carefully decided on alternative methods. All students in this city who should participate in the make-up exam this year may take the original school's graduation exam at their original school and make up for the subjects they failed in the joint entrance examination. If the original school's exam period has passed, the make-up exam students may request the original school to schedule a special make-up exam and report it to the Bureau for sending personnel to supervise the exam. After the make-up exam is completed, the school should report the results, and after verification and approval, the certificate will be issued. Students from various provinces and cities who are entrusted by this Bureau to take the exam should report to the Bureau within two weeks after the start of the next semester and wait for the scheduled make-up exam. After the make-up exam is completed, the exam papers will be sent to the original entrusting provincial and municipal agencies for re-evaluation. This announcement is hereby made for your information."

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Compilation of the Middle School Teaching Progress Table Is About to Be Completed; The First Draft Will Be Completed Before the End of This Month; It Can Be Trial Implemented Starting Next Semester 182

In order to standardize the teaching progress of various subjects in public and private middle schools in the city, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau specially hired 39 people including Shao Jialin, Wang Jimei, Zhang Yousan, Chen Duanzhi, and Li Dihua as members to form a committee to compile the middle school teaching progress table. They have held several group meetings and discussed in detail, and have decided on the principles of compilation: 1. Take the week as the unit; 2. The teaching materials should be concise; 3. The details should be the minimum; 4. Pay attention to local special teaching materials; 5. The compilation order should follow the standards issued by the Ministry as much as possible; 6. Avoid repetition of junior and middle school teaching materials. It is learned that the first draft will be completed before the end of this month, and it can be trial implemented starting next semester.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (1) (5) (1) 183

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"I don't believe you would do it. You sometimes like to fight, but you don't lie. I don't believe you would steal," said Nat, shaking his head to show that it was impossible.

"I have done worse things. I used to lie like mad; now I think it is too much trouble. When I ran away from Mr. Bell's, I stole things from the garden to eat on the way; so you see I am a bad lot," said Dan, in the rough, impudent tone which he was lately trying so hard to get rid of.

"Oh, Dan! Don't say it was you! I'd rather it had been any other boy," cried Nat, so full of sorrow that Dan was touched, and involuntarily showed it, for he turned away with a queer look on his face, though he only answered:

"I don't want to say anything about it. But you needn't fret; we'll get along all right; you see if we don't."

His face and his manner gave Nat a new idea; he clasped his hands tight, and said eagerly:

"I think you know who did it. If you do, make him tell, Dan. They all hate me without any reason, and it is very hard. I don't think I can bear it much longer. If I had any place to go, I'd leave Plumfield, which I love so much, and go somewhere else; but I haven't got such a body as you, nor your courage; so I must stay and wait till somebody tells them I did not lie."

Commercial News

Finance Gold Prices Rise After Low Prices Trigger Buying Interest; Gold Loan Collateral—Monthly Interest at 7% 187

From Weak to Strong—Rise of $1.10 188

Yesterday's gold market started weak, but buying interest picked up due to low prices, enabling a rebound. The overall trend fluctuated around the $40 mark. As the settlement date approached, the market remained relatively stable. In the early morning, with overseas silver markets in the UK and US closed, the forward silver price in Montreal rose slightly by one to three and a half points. Exchange rates remained high. The London gold price fell by one penny. Reports indicated that the Central Bank had initiated gold loan collateral, but the monthly interest rate was as high as 7% (around $8 for forward contracts). Although concerns about the settlement date were slightly alleviated, the US Treasury Department was still reportedly in contact with us to purchase silver, with the first batch priced at 65 cents per ounce. Selling pressure remained difficult to suppress. Off-exchange trading opened lower, falling to $37.80 due to supply from Fuxingyong, but Yuanyangyong Qingfayong Dadecheng Huixiang and others took advantage of the low prices to buy, pushing the price up to over $40. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with no changes in the UK and US. The customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard gold loan collateral price was lowered to $1145.90. Dadecheng sold gold bars at high prices, causing the price to fall back below $40. The morning opened with low prices, and the trend continued downward due to oversupply. Central and Jiaotong banks seized the opportunity to buy at low prices, and short sellers covered their positions, allowing the price to rebound above $40. At this point, HSBC's official exchange rates remained unchanged, and banks traded forward contracts, stabilizing market sentiment. The price fluctuated around the $40 mark, but as buying interest gradually recovered, the price soon rebounded again. Large players supplied gold bars at high prices, and prices gradually stabilized after reaching a high point. The silver balancing tax remained unchanged. There was still much fluctuation, and market sentiment gradually turned uncertain. Later, the market lacked sustained buying interest and was once pressured by sellers, falling back below $40. However, due to large short sellers covering their positions, the situation stabilized at noon. The after-market was slightly weak, but was able to rebound after opening. Regarding the news about silver exports, Reuters' report was partially acknowledged. Banks bought US dollars and sold British pounds, stabilizing exchange rates, which also led to price increases throughout the city. HSBC bought US dollars, and Indian silver prices were reported to have shrunk by 10 annas. Buying interest increased slightly, causing a rebound, but prices leveled off again after reaching a high point. The forward premium yesterday fell to around $4.50, equivalent to a monthly interest rate of 7%. This settlement period is still expected to see a premium of around $8, mainly because the Central Bank's gold loan collateral requires an interest rate of 7%. The day's market situation is recorded below:

Qiafeng Yongquan Dadecheng Huixiang Dingkang all bought at low prices, gradually raising the price to $40.60. HSBC's official exchange rates for the UK and US remained unchanged, and market sentiment was stable. Dada Fuxingyong still sold, lowering the price to $0.x. Dadecheng Yuanchang Yong took the opportunity to sell at high prices, lowering the price to $0.6. Xianghe Fuxingyong Huixiang bought again, raising the price to $2.40. Dadecheng took the opportunity to sell at high prices, falling to $1.30. Huixiang Fuxingyong Houyu bought gold bars, raising the price to $1.90. The increase in Shanghai's British exchange rate shows a consistent trend with London silver prices, which has been a unique phenomenon since the beginning of this year. This is different from last year when China's foreign exchange rates moved away from silver prices. However, this is only a difference in degree. If Shanghai's foreign exchange rates are compared with London silver prices, there is still a significant distance in exchange rates, which is why the collection of the balancing tax is still important.

Since the United States implemented silver nationalization last August, China's silver has flowed out in large quantities as silver prices have risen. However, this year, the outflow of silver has come to an end, and there is even a surplus, which is clear from the table below.

Comparison of Shanghai's Silver Import and Export in 1935 (Note 5)

However, the smuggling of silver cannot be reflected in the table above, so the actual situation is not so simple.

The reasons why the outflow of silver has stopped are:

Due to the collection of the balancing tax, it is no longer profitable to export silver.

China's foreign exchange rates have gradually risen, and the difference between foreign exchange rates and silver prices is small, so it is also unprofitable to export silver.

The China's central bank and Shanghai foreign banks have reached a gentleman's agreement, reducing the manipulation of foreign banks.

Fourth,

Those in the economic sector who are directly related to the rise and fall of foreign exchange rates are none other than import and export trade. Let us try to observe the situation of this year's exchange rate changes and import and export trade: (Note 6)

Trade has a seasonal relationship, so it is impossible to observe its general trend in the short term. However, foreign exchange rates have a direct impact on it. Even if the time is very short, a general idea can be seen. The increase in China's foreign exchange rates indicates an increase in the purchasing power of China's currency. In theory, China's imports should greatly increase. However, looking at the table above, although imports gradually increased from January to May, after removing the seasonal impact, how much of the increase is due to the increase in currency purchasing power cannot be immediately determined. According to recent customs reports, the total value of China's import and export trade in the first half of this year decreased compared with the same period in previous years. The total value of imports decreased by 24,394,541 yuan compared with the same period last year, and exports decreased by 9,175,041 yuan compared with the same period last year (Note 7). The increase in imports cannot be achieved simply by increasing the purchasing power of currency. If the purchasing power of currency increases on one side, but the social economy of the other side is sluggish and the general purchasing power is low, then consumption will inevitably not rise. This should be taken as a warning by those who use dumping policies to seize markets in other countries.

Silk and Tea: Drastic Decline in Chinese Tea Exports to the United States 197

The United States has historically been the main consumer market for Chinese tea exports. In recent years, due to competition from Indian, Ceylon, Japanese, and Javanese teas, the volume of Chinese tea exports to the United States has decreased from 400,000 chests to 100,000 chests. Last year, due to various factors, exports of Chinese Ping-Shui green tea and both Hunan-Hubei Qimen-Ningzhou black tea to the United States fell sharply to 65,000 chests. The reason for this decline is attributed to the abundant harvests and dumping of cheap tea from India, Ceylon, Japan, and Taiwan in the past year. Furthermore, the quality of Chinese black and green tea has not been pure, and the color and processing methods have deteriorated compared to previous years, which is also a major factor. If reforms are not urgently pursued, the position of Chinese tea in the American market will inevitably gradually decline.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 199

— (Tie Wu)

The white-faced scholar behind the stage, once he runs to the front, will put on the makeup of black-faced Zhang Fei or red-faced Guan Gong. A person in the mother's womb is like a white-faced scholar behind the stage. Once out of the womb, onto the stage of the universe, because he has to perform a play of life, he either enters black or red. The former purity will never be found again.

Cherish time, starting with every minute and every second, because a human life of a hundred years is entirely accumulated from many minutes and seconds.

Grasp the present five minutes, do not fail the future five minutes, do not waste the past five minutes. Encourage and strive like this every moment, and great achievements will be firmly built on this encouragement and effort. The needle on the clock, as long as the spring is tightened from time to time, it will always move forward. A person's life only occupies a section of the entire process. To make this section shine with extraordinary brilliance, one must make unremitting efforts throughout life.

Before the sun and the earth collapse, spring, summer, autumn, and winter go and come again, endlessly circulating. Life, however, is gone and never returns. "Do not idly waste your youthful head, only to weep in vain."

Elegant Chat About Love 200

— Yong Cai

Enveloped in this atmosphere of economic downturn, news of the pleasure quarters in the north is also becoming bleak. The playboys and young men who used to enjoy seeking pleasure are now, due to their depleted wallets, only able to stroke their large coat pockets and sigh in vain.

Although the beginnings of examining prostitutes were initiated by Guan Zhong's "300 female quarters," it was not until the Ming Dynasty that it gradually flourished. At that time, all self-proclaimed romantic literati liked to visit Jin Chan. When in high spirits, they would write several poems and pass them on to friends. Therefore, poems about prostitutes were most abundant in the Ming Dynasty. If we were to carefully collect them and compile a "Three Hundred Poems on Prostitutes," it would indeed be a magnificent masterpiece, not letting Tang poetry monopolize the beauty of the past.

Our country's circumstances differ between the north and the south, so habits also differ. Even small actions reveal personality unintentionally. Take prostitutes for example: Southern prostitutes are accustomed to pouring flattery and playing tricks, using smooth and hypocritical means to win over their lovers. Northern prostitutes, on the other hand, are straightforward and value loyalty. Once they become intimate with a stranger, they treat each other with sincerity and righteousness. This is a very obvious and definite fact.

Lower-class brothels in the north include several types such as "Mo Hei" (touching in the dark) and "Ji Mao Wo" (chicken feather nest), which are places where coolies and rickshaw pullers seek pleasure, paying only a few dozen copper coins per encounter. It is said that the facilities of "Ji Mao Wo" are even simpler than "Mo Hei." In the room, besides a few prostitutes, there is only a pit, with some chicken feathers piled on it, which serves as the "waiting place." This was told to me by a veteran of northern pleasure quarters.

Chen Dasheng of the Ming Dynasty wrote a song mocking northern prostitutes, and although it is only a few dozen sentences long, it fully demonstrates the ability to satirize and describe. It is specially recorded here for your amusement: "A sound of mules and horses passing in front of the door, dust flying, where is the fragrant hoof of a horse returning after treading flowers? Cotton-padded jacket, cotton-padded pants, cotton-padded skirt, bulging, where is the thin silk dress first tried in the spring breeze? Raw scallions, raw garlic, raw chives, pickled and dirty, where is the fragrant mouth grease of secret whispers late at night? Opening her mouth to sing of wronged families, a crooked tune, where is the song of Du Wei's daughter in the spring breeze? Raising a cup to eat shaojiu together, unbearable, where is the fragrant tulip wine of Lanling? A loose bun two feet high on her head, a barbarian girl, where is the high bun and cloud-like hair of a palace style? Where is the rain and clouds, a dirt pit, where is the mandarin duck sleeping in a gilded tent at night? Five qian one liang, the head is held high, then forgotten, where is marrying Liu Lang better than Ruan Lang?"

Legal Suicide 201

— Wei Jing

Suicide is a sin, we often hear this. Suicide is a criminal act, this is also a law in civilized countries around the world. But in London, there is a "Quick Death Association," successfully organized by several physicians, jurists, priests, and others of standing. Its purpose is to protect those qualified to commit suicide from leaving this world. Their view is that for people suffering from incurable diseases, rather than letting them linger in bed, slowly and painfully heading towards death, it is better to grant them the legal right to quick death, so that they suffer less from the pain of dying.

Weak Animals Surrounded by Enemies 202

Under this goal, one of the founders of the association, the famous physician Sir Moynihan, is preparing to submit a law to Parliament, allowing those who meet the conditions to request quick death, to end their lives in a simple and painless way. The conditions that must be met for quick death are suffering from an incurable disease. In terms of procedures, a written statement of willingness to die must be signed in person. At the time of signing, two of the closest relatives and two qualified doctors must be present to witness and must also sign the death warrant to prove that the person wishing to die is indeed suffering from an incurable disease. This kind of open and legal suicide is truly a rare and ancient event. Suicide with legal protection, those who commit suicide can calmly go to their death, this may not be a gospel for those who commit suicide. But looking at the organization's essence of this Quick Death Association, it is completely based on humanitarianism, so the qualifications of those seeking death are limited to those with incurable diseases. It is known that those who commit suicide due to economic oppression, failed love, etc., really have no need to commit suicide. This point, I hope those who are momentarily impulsive and tired of the world, pay attention to.

Little Western Heaven 203

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23: Arguing Vigorously in the Room to File a Lawsuit, Pouring Wine to Renew Old Friendships, Benefits Can Make One Forget Grievances

Just as he said this, the curtain was lifted, and a person in student attire walked in. He took off his hat and nodded to him, saying, "Mr. Jia, I am very presumptuous! But this is the profession of a newspaper reporter, please forgive me." Jia Duocai frowned and said, "Making friends is always welcome, but I am a businessman. I'm afraid there are no materials for you to interview, right?" The visitor laughed, "Finding news materials doesn't necessarily require visiting important people. I believe that Mr. Jia can tell us the truth, then there will be a lot of material." As he spoke, he rubbed his hands and sat down, as if to indicate a little hesitation. But as soon as he was seated, he took out a small diary from his pocket. While flipping it open, he laughed and said, "I just met Commissioner Lan's wife, and she mentioned that there is a problem on Mr. Jia." When Jia Duocai came in, he already knew what he meant, always wanting to muddle through. Now that the other party honestly took out his diary, it was inconvenient to say that this was absolutely not the case, so he forced a smile and said, "A person working outside, taking a temporary family member, it doesn't count for much. Canceling the temporary family member, it's even less worth anything?" The visitor laughed and said, "Does Mr. Jia mean that you don't want Ms. Zhu to come back?" Jia Duocai thought for a while, laughed, "How can she be called Ms. Zhu? You, sir, have raised her personality too high." The visitor laughed, "This is just a casual way of addressing her, you don't have to mind it. If she just leaves you and goes home, what attitude will you take towards her?" Jia Duocai shook his head and said, "I don't want to express any opinions, please forgive me." The visitor laughed, "Mr. Jia is probably preparing to file a lawsuit. But this matter has already involved the women's issue. Those ladies and misses have already regarded Mr. Jia's marriage problem not as a personal matter but as the honor and disgrace of the entire women's circle. The law is nothing more than human feelings. With these women coming forward, the court will have to consider carefully when judging." After saying this, he smiled lightly and looked at Jia Duocai, waiting for his reply. (891)

World Rare News

Firsthand Observations of Abyssinia 204

— Ji Yun

Since the Italo-Abyssinian War, the country of Abyssinia has been known far and wide. A black country that everyone looks down on dares to confront Mussolini's mighty army, giving the weak and small nations a chance to exhale. Of course, although defeated, it is glorious. The following is a conversation with Mr. Tsuchida Yutaka, the Japanese foreign affairs secretary. He visited Abyssinia last year for inspection, and what he said may be more accurate.

To get to Abyssinia, the most convenient way is to take a ship to Djibouti on the French Somali Coast, where there is a railway that leads directly to the Abyssinian capital. Starting from the station, the road is all desert, not even three-foot shrubs, and black-brown rocks cannot be seen. The train is barely crawling up the plateau, and under the strong sunlight, without black glasses, it is impossible to see anything. Even with the electric fan on, it is still so hot that you want to drink water all the time. When you get to Kineidu in Abyssinia, you are already five thousand feet above sea level. All around are green trees, and the weather is gradually getting cooler. Further south is the village of Awash, full of malarial mosquitoes, so you must use a mosquito net. At night, you can only hear the wind down the mountain and the sound of wolves barking, which is extremely scary. The land gradually rises, and the temperature gradually decreases. When you get near the Abyssinian capital, you can no longer bear a shirt, so you have to put on a coat. In the car, you can see purple valleys all around, with a group of white buildings in the middle. That is the Abyssinian capital, eight thousand feet above sea level.

When the train reaches the Abyssinian capital, there is suddenly thunder and lightning, and a heavy rain, which is a special product of Abyssinia. From May to mid-September is the rainy season, with at least one or two rains a day. After the rain clears and the sun comes out, people wear thick shoulder cloths to protect themselves from the sunlight. The Abyssinian capital is very high, so the summer is as mild as spring and autumn in the northern temperate zone, but the air is thin, which is a drawback.

Abyssinia is called Ethiopia, in eastern Africa, with an area of 350,000 square miles, larger than Japan itself. Although the population is said to be ten million, it is not accurate. The history of the country is nearly four thousand years. At that time, the Queen of Sheba, who came on a long expedition from Arabia, became the ruler of Abyssinia. Because she admired the hero Solomon on the Mediterranean coast, she personally visited him. One night she returned and gave birth to a prince, who was Emperor Menelik I of Abyssinia. So to this day, the people of Abyssinia still boast: "We are the descendants of the prince born of the great king and queen." From Menelik I onwards, there was an imperial autocracy of about two thousand years. Later, the heroes were divided and rebelled one after another. In the 19th century, Menelik II restored Abyssinia, unifying the country with the help of many Italians, so he ceded the northern coastal land to Italy. Also, due to British and French intervention, he ceded the northeast coastal land to Britain and France, while he did not have a way to the sea. So Menelik II can be said to be a restoration, but also a troublemaker who led the wolf into the house. Later, there was indeed a rebellion, and the civil war did not stop. The great Christian masters rose up to establish Menelik II's niece, Zewditu, as queen, and the current Emperor of Abyssinia, Haile Selassie, served as regent. In 1923, with French assistance, she joined the League of Nations. In 1930, the Queen collapsed, and Haile Selassie continued to hold the national position. The Queen's name is Menen, and she has three sons and two daughters. Abyssinia is completely a feudal system. The chiefs of various places are recruiting soldiers, and they gather in the Abyssinian capital every three years to pay their respects. One-third of the country is the Amhara people, who are the true Abyssinian bloodline. They all believe in Christianity and are officials, scholars, and warriors. In addition, there are Muslims and completely ignorant black slaves, who can only be enslaved.

People are martial and warlike, which is the traditional atmosphere. At banquets, they use strange instruments to accompany the dance with swords in song. Their songs mostly describe the story of the victory over Italy in the Battle of Adwa. Because their ancestors had the glory of a great victory over Italy, the people and warriors all despise Roman warriors. In fact, today's Italy is far from what it used to be. Even Britain and France see it as a headache, but the people of Abyssinia still think that they can defeat the Italian army like their ancestors.

The etiquette between friends is very important. When they meet on the road, they often greet each other. Sometimes two people embrace, and two black beards face, rubbing each other. The upper class eats beef and mutton, while the lower class only eats some salty pasta.

Notes on What I Saw 205

— (Yangtze River)

At dusk, the cold wind was blowing sharply. I walked shivering across the intersection of Connaught Road and Jiaozhou Road, but I saw a group of people gathered near the mailbox, shouting, scolding, and laughing. Looking closely, it was a woman who was being bullied.

That woman was no more than twenty-two or three years old, and she was still good-looking. Her clothes were not tattered either, but she kept begging from the windows of the houses where Westerners lived. The patrol came to interfere, pulled her to run, but she refused. He drove her back, but she said, "Where do I have a home!" Then she cried loudly again!

A ticket inspector came down from the bus. Seeing that it was a woman, he used a flashlight to illuminate her face for a long time. Although she was a little shy and annoyed, she did not have the courage to protest!

In the Chinese dictionary, there is only ridicule, no sympathy.

Record of the Fourth National Physicians' Association Congress 208

The Fourth National Physicians' Association Congress of National Physician Representatives has already been held at the Xuan Palace Hotel in Hankou, starting on January 1st of this year. Representatives from Kunming, Wuzhou, Chongqing, Ganxian, Shenyang, Beiping, Changsha, Qingdao, Anqing, Shanghai, Nanjing, Wuhu, Hangzhou, Rugao, Jinsha, Jiangyin, Zhenjiang, Yongjia, Lanzhou, Xuchang, Hefei, Shayang, and other places, as well as representatives from the Hankou and Hubei Provincial Physicians' Associations, totaling over 300 people, attended. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM on New Year's Day. Representatives from the local Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Health, the Provincial Government, the Municipal Government, the Garrison Headquarters, the Department of Civil Affairs, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the National Lawyers' Association, the National Accountants' Association, the National New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, the Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, the local New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, and others, all attended and delivered speeches. At 11:00 AM, a preparatory meeting was held, and the rules of procedure were passed. Xu Naili, Cai Yumen, Chen Fangzhi, Hu Ding'an, Di Huasan, Shen Zhongling, Xu Zuyi, Yang Boru, Chuai Zhiran, Zhang Dongting, and Zhang Senyu were elected as the presidium. In addition, a review committee was organized to review the proposals in groups, including Dai Xiamin, Zhao Jisheng, Zhang Dingmin, Jian Hui, Shao Jiyun, Jiang Huchen, and You Zhiyong, seven members of the medical administration group, convened by Dai Xiamin; Yang Yusheng, Zhou Zhenyun, Chen Weitang, Li Ziheng, and Zhang Shibin, five members of the organization group, convened by Yang Yusheng; Jiang Zhenxun, Cheng Hanzhang, Hu Jingou, Zhu Hongzhi, Wen Yiqi, Lu Yongchun, and Chi Zhongjiu, seven members of the advisory group, convened by Jiang Zhenxun; Zhou Mingyu, Gu Nankui, Hao Juemin, Ling Chaoqun, and Shi Ruxiong, five members of the general affairs group, convened by Zhou Mingyu. At noon, a public banquet was held by the Hubei Provincial Physicians' Association and the Hankou Municipal Physicians' Association. In the afternoon, the first formal meeting was held, and the draft of the Physicians' Association Law was passed and submitted to the government for adoption. The proposal to organize a health cooperative, which was discussed at the previous congress, was re-submitted for discussion, and it was resolved to submit a request to the government to promote it. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM. In the evening, a public banquet was held by Wuzhou Xinya Xinyi and three pharmaceutical factories. At 9:00 AM on the second day, the second formal meeting was held, and the following resolutions were passed: To request the authorities to examine and verify practical medical talents in order to popularize hygiene and relieve the public; and to propose that the government administer medical affairs construction in education by regions. The above two cases were discussed together and resolved to be amended and passed. To request the Congress to suggest that the Legislative Yuan not include the right to practice medicine in commercial activities when formulating the Physicians' Law, in order to limit foreign doctors from practicing medicine in our country. To request the government to promptly promulgate regulations for foreign doctors to practice medicine. Also, for doctors in church hospitals, they should also be registered uniformly in accordance with the Provisional Regulations for Physicians. The above three cases were discussed together and resolved to be passed. To request the government to strictly prohibit old-style doctors from indiscriminately administering injections and drugs; and to strictly prohibit people from hiding and using injection needles in order to value people's lives and benefit the ban on addiction. The above two cases were discussed together and resolved to be passed. When various regions promulgate separate medical and health laws and regulations, they should solicit or refer to the opinions of the local physicians' associations. To request the amendment of Article 4, Section 1 of the Provisional Regulations for Physicians in order to protect the public rights of physicians. A plan to resolve disputes with patients in business; and to request the government to issue a general order to public security authorities nationwide that they must not abuse their authority in the event of business disputes. The above four cases were discussed together and resolved to be passed. To suggest that the central government announce the Physicians' Law to consolidate their duties. It was resolved to hand it over to the next executive committee to organize a special committee to properly draft the provisions for government adoption. To request a joint agreement on a unified standard for examining opium smokers and request the authorities to implement it nationwide. It was resolved to establish another special committee to handle it. Local governments should promote occupational health guidance to enhance the working capacity of the people. It was resolved to notify all member organizations to start with promotion. To request the government to promote eugenics to strengthen the nation. It was resolved: (A) Before marriage, both men and women should first obtain a health certificate from a doctor as an initial step in eugenics; (B) People suffering from mental illness should undergo artificial sterilization after identification; (C) Promote maternal and infant health. To request the government to create more medical talents and increase health agencies. It was resolved: (A) In remote provinces and regions, each county should select at least one or two publicly funded medical students each year; (B) In densely populated areas with incomplete health facilities, health services should be popularized, with at least one health agency in each administrative supervisory area. At noon, a banquet was held by Yang Yongtai, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, in the auditorium of the Provincial Government. After the banquet, I went to Luojia Mountain to visit Wuhan University. The school prepared tea and snacks to welcome us. To request the government to re-define the education regulations for midwives and nurses and strictly define the scope of their business. To suggest that the government restrict the misuse of the title of doctor in order to value life and correct public opinion. At 8:00 PM, a public banquet was held by sixteen new pharmaceutical industry groups in Hankou. At 9:00 AM on the third day, the fourth meeting was held and the motion was passed. To formulate a work outline for the next session of the Association and ask for approval and implementation. Approved with amendments. To propose to establish a cooperative for the sale of medicines and equipment. Resolved to be handled by local member organizations at their discretion. To train rescue teams and set up a health materials factory as soon as possible to deal with emergencies. The principles were approved and handed over to the next Executive Committee for handling. To request that the venue for the Fifth Congress be set in Chongqing, Sichuan. Resolved to be referred to the next Executive Committee for reference. To request the formulation of a charter for the Physicians' Association in various regions for common compliance. Resolved to be handled by the next Executive Committee. Resolved to hand it over to the next Executive Committee to form a Physicians' Creed Committee to handle it. To request the National Physicians' Association to issue membership certificates and formulate membership badges for members to store, hang, and wear. It was resolved that the National Physicians' Association would print and distribute membership certificates for member organizations to hang. The badges will be issued to members in various regions to wear. The cost of the certificates and badges will be paid according to the actual number. At the end of the meeting, executive and supervisory committee members were elected. As a result, Xu Naili, Cai Yumen, Yu Yunxiu, Chen Fangzhi, Jiang Zhenzhu, Zai Qizhang, Niu Huisheng, Xia Shenchu, and Zhang Senyu were elected as executive committee members. Common Sense Q&A About Diseases 209

— Cheng Hanzhang

(76) Gallstone Colic (Part 2)

(Q) What are some of the complications of gallstone disease patients?

(A) There are many complications of gallstone disease: including gallbladder hydrops, cholemia, cancer, inflammation of the bile duct and gallbladder, portal vein, etc., and peritonitis.

(Q) How does gallbladder hydrops occur?

(A) When the cystic duct is blocked, gallbladder hydrops or hydrops of the gallbladder may occur without jaundice.

(Q) How does cholemia occur?

(A) When the bile duct is blocked, jaundice occurs first, followed by cholemia, which leads to bleeding, digestive disorders, and decreased heart function, eventually leading to lethargy and death.

(Q) How does cancer occur?

(A) Cancer occurs due to constant irritation from gallstones.

(Q) How do complications such as cholangitis occur?

(A) After pathogens invade, they can cause cholangitis, cholecystitis, portal vein inflammation, and even liver abscesses. There can also be compression necrosis of the biliary tract, scar stenosis, etc.

(Q) How does peritonitis occur?

(A) Peritonitis occurs because gallstones penetrate the stomach, intestines, colon, or abdominal cavity.

(Q) What are the diagnostic methods for gallstone disease?

(A) Diagnosing gallstone disease depends on determining whether it is colic, enlargement of the liver and gallbladder, sensitivity in that area, fever, jaundice after an attack, and proof of gallstones in the stool, etc.

(Q) What diseases should gallstone disease be distinguished from?

(A) It should be distinguished from gastric spasms, gastric ulcers, duodenal ulcers, intestinal colic, renal colic, wandering kidney, diaphragmatic pleurisy, pancreatic colic, pancreatic necrosis, appendicitis, cirrhosis, etc.

(Q) What else should be paid attention to?

(A) In addition, attention should be paid to congestive gallbladder. In this case, colic can occur even if there are no gallstones in the gallbladder.

(Q) What is the prognosis of gallstone disease?

(A) If it is a typical gallstone colic attack, there is no danger. However, if it is combined with other diseases, it is not optimistic. If attacks recur, it will progress to chronic obstructive jaundice, peritonitis, or bile duct cancer, etc.

(Q) In the treatment of gallstone disease, what should be done during a colic attack?

(A) At this time, the patient should be ordered to rest quietly in bed, and cold or warm compresses should be applied to the gallbladder area. Food should avoid fatty and stimulating foods.

(Q) Can painkillers be used?

(A) If the colic is very severe, various anesthetics can be used. Injection or oral administration are both acceptable.

(Q) What common medicines can be used to clear the bile?

(A) Medicines that promote bile excretion, such as ferrous sulfate and artificial spring salt, can be taken orally.

(Q) What should be done if these methods are ineffective?

(A) Only surgical operation.

Methods to Prevent Influenza (Commonly Known as the Common Cold) 210

— Original by Prof. Dr. W. Berger et al., Translated and Abridged by Chen Shengbai

(Chen) For those who are prone to colds, such as infants, pregnant women, postpartum women, the elderly, patients in the recovery period, those who have just undergone surgery, those with rickets, scoliosis, and those with circulatory diseases, patients with scarlet fever and measles, visiting patients should be prohibited or they should stay away from epidemic areas. As for the use of protective masks, isolation, and taking quinine in poor environments, many misfortunes can be avoided.

(Ji) Refer to Prausnitz's report. During the flu epidemic, the waiting time in hospitals, clinics, and official waiting rooms should be shortened as much as possible. Especially in hospitals, the opportunity for infection during the waiting period can lead to rampant transmission of colds.

(Geng) Hospital management also plays an important role in group prevention of the flu. Like

A Hospital authorities should be obligated to report that hospitalization of a flu patient poses a risk of infection. Therefore, hospital authorities should always be concerned about it.

B Patient isolation

C Seriously ill patients, especially those with pneumonia or patients who have died of pneumonia, should have their wards thoroughly disinfected. Because there is a close relationship between the flu and pneumonia.

D General prohibition of visiting patients Any disease, or at least a dangerous disease, should be prevented from spreading. Of course, the flu is no exception. When it is unavoidable, as mentioned above, protective masks should be worn, fingers should be cleaned, and quinine should be taken internally.

E Sincere publicity and guidance, constant monitoring, rapid information. The use of quinine and protective masks. Ordinary people also have an obligation to implement them effectively. Doctors and nurses in hospitals are already in a guiding position. We should intensify the work that should be done.

There is no doubt that the combined effect of the above methods is effective. However, the individual's energy, the thoroughness of implementation, and the adaptation of organizational technology and methods to us also have a great impact on infection prevention.

(Yi) Prevention of Disease Method

The chances of flu transmission are so high. And it is so difficult to prevent its transmission. So its infection cannot be avoided in case of emergency. After being infected, one should pay attention to the following guidelines on how to prevent the onset of disease.

Individual Prevention of Disease

(Zi) One should strictly guard against cold, overwork, malnutrition, dust, smoking and other factors that can cause the onset of disease.

(Chou) Quinine Oral Prevention Method Drug prevention is most effective, and has been proven by scholars' experiments. Up to now. Quinine is still recognized as the number one. Quinine for the flu is the same as for malaria. Has value in prevention and treatment.

A Quinine prevention method time and duration

Once the epidemic period begins. If you take quinine orally. Until no new cases are reported. Of course it's the best way. As for sporadic or persistent epidemics. It is also necessary to continue taking it. Others for professional reasons. Or those who have intermittent flu attacks should take it all year round or from December 1 to April 4.

The so-called short-term prevention method. That is, emergency measures for unavoidable visits, minor colds among colleagues, and gatherings in epidemic areas.

B The choice of drugs should conform to the principles of comfort, ease of administration, and no bad taste. Such as Quinisal (Cbin, BisalicBoehringer 0.25)．Chininperlen＂Zimmer＂(0.05-0.1 und 0.2 ChinHydrrochl puriss) etc. As for whether it is more effective to take quinine alone or to take it with salicylic acid (Acid Salicyl) preparations. Still needs to be reported separately.

C Dosage has large doses. 0.25-0.5 daily. There are small amounts. 0.5 daily.

D Side effects According to the prevention method of quinine and salicylic acid at 0.25 that we use. There are very few side effects.

(Yin) Prevention of Disease with Other Drugs

A. Kleinert's Salicyl．＆Urotropin

B H. Berg's iodine prevention method

C Spitta's Protargol nasal drip method. All have considerable effects.

D Due to oral hygiene (gargling with Panflavin, Formamint, etc. and washing with disinfectant water), the resulting effects are probably not very reliable.

(Mao) Although the special immune prevention method has not been scientifically and rigorously proven. But it has value in use. Unfortunately, the lasting effect of this method cannot be extended very much. So it is necessary to repeat the vaccination.

The so-called mixed vaccine. Refers to many dead bacteria that can cause colds. According to general experience. Seems to have no great effect

Group Prevention of Disease

The group prevention method to prevent the occurrence of colds. It is not only limited to the rules of infection prevention mentioned above. At the same time, the government should also. Overall planning. To study how to avoid the causes of disease. Like heating equipment. Nutrition supply, etc.

Conclusion

Although there are more than just these prevention methods for the flu. But if you can implement the main guidelines mentioned above, you will definitely be able to reduce the onset of colds. Reduce the infectious power of colds. Finally. I want to solemnly declare again. Is that in addition to protective masks, banning visits, isolation and other methods. An easy-to-use oral quinine prevention method. For infection prevention, especially disease prevention. Because it has a definitive effect. Therefore, I would like to give a strong introduction to readers again. (The End)

Medicinal Plants of Domestic Origin (Continued) 211

— Zhou Mengbai

(11) Safflower Carthamus Tinctorius, L. Farbercistal, Saflor (German) Safflower (English)

(Plant) Originally from Egypt, it can be cultivated everywhere, an annual herb. The stem is one meter high, the leaves are alternate, broadly lanceolate, and the edges are serrated with sharp spines, and the tips are sharp. Terminal capitulum, the edge of the involucre is also serrated with sharp spines, and its shape is similar to that of thistle flowers.

(Crude drug) Safflower Flas Carthami is the dried product collected from its corolla. The corolla is tubular, the tip is split, and it is one centimeter long. The fresh one is yellow-red on the outside, and the old one is reddish-brown or dark brown. It has a unique and mild aroma and a slightly bitter taste.

Plate Safflower is the red color that has been pressed and dried. This product is usually in the shape of a square plate, with a width of five to six square centimeters and a thickness of two to three millimeters, and is dark red. My country produces a lot of it and often imports it to Japan, making it a good product among safflowers.

(Ingredients) The flower contains yellow pigment (Saflorgelb C24H30O15) and red pigment (Carthamin C H22C10). The glycoside of red pigment, its seeds contain 20-30% fatty oil.

(Medicinal) In old prescriptions, safflower is a medicine for returning to women and promoting menstruation. It must be soaked in wine when taken. It can also be made into edible red, which is a harmless coloring pigment for women's makeup and snacks.

Manufacturing method of edible red Soak safflower in water for one day and night to fully remove the dissolved yellow pigment, and use ash juice to dissolve the red pigment, soak ramie in the liquid, add dilute sulfuric acid or plum vinegar (leachate of black plum), so that the red substance settles on the ramie, wash it in water for a considerable time, and then dissolve it with a small amount of ash juice, and add plum vinegar again, so that all the red substances it contains are precipitated? Finally, filter and dry it with silk cloth to obtain it. Dry red can be obtained by filtering and manufacturing dry safflower. 0.76%

Common Sense Q&A About Teeth (16) 212

— Lin Jianxian

Section 3 Alveolar Pyorrhea

(Question 87) What are the symptoms of non-infectious periodontitis?

(Answer) The common symptoms have already been explained in question 78 above. All the symptoms are not as severe as those of acute infectious diseases. However, the periodontal membrane becomes mildly congested and inflamed, and the teeth are slightly raised and sore. However, if it is not cured for a long time, it is easy to be infected and cause suppuration, and the symptoms become severe.

(Question 88) What kind of disease is alveolar pyorrhea?

(Answer) Alveolar pyorrhea, commonly known as "ya gan" in our country. Although it also has inflammation of the periodontal membrane, it is completely different from what was discussed in Section 2 above. The teeth themselves are mostly intact and there are no changes. However, the alveolar bone gradually atrophies, and there is often a kind of pus flowing out of the gums. If not treated, the teeth will gradually loosen and fall out naturally. Moreover, after this disease occurs, it is often not limited to one tooth, and neighboring teeth often show the same symptoms, eventually falling out. This disease is very common, and many teeth are lost because of it. Therefore, it can be considered the two most common and most harmful types of dental diseases together with tooth decay and pulpitis and periodontitis caused by tooth decay. Most of the work of dentists is spent on treating these two types of diseases

(Question 89) What are the causes of alveolar pyorrhea?

(Answer) The causes are very complicated and there is still no definite cause. Most of them are due to the lime contained in the saliva and food debris, etc., adhering to the neck of the teeth. After accumulation for a long time, it gradually hardens into a layer of dirt like stone. This is called dental calculus (it can also be formed by the accumulation of blood excretions). Because of the stimulation of this dental calculus, the gums will become congested and inflamed, and after a long time, they will separate from the teeth to form a sac. Germs and dirt invade, and pus leakage occurs. But it can also be caused by systemic diseases. Such as syphilis, diabetes, lung disease, neurasthenia, etc.

(Question 90) How many types of alveolar pyorrhea can be divided into?

(Answer) It can be divided into three types, and the symptoms of each type are slightly different.

(Question 91) What are the symptoms of the first type?

(Answer) There is a circle of black and hard dental calculus around the neck of the teeth. The edge of the gums is red, swollen and inflamed. This symptom is relatively mild and is the initial stage of alveolar pyorrhea. Most sacs have not formed; most have no pus.

A Simple Explanation of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (79) 213

— Hu Jiayan

Section 6: Specialized Stimulus Therapy - Tuberculin

What tuberculin is, and its value in the diagnosis of this disease, have been described in detail in Chapter 8 of this book! But besides diagnosis, it also has great value in the treatment of this disease: many people even claim that if used properly, it can be considered a specialized and effective treatment! We know that tuberculin is made from tubercle bacillus toxin, hence the name tuberculin; if injected into the human body, it causes great changes in the inflammatory state of the lesion, the slightest being an increase in redness and swelling of the lesion, and more severe cases may cause the lesion to collapse. Therefore, in principle, it can directly reach the lesion; and it cannot be treated in the same way as other methods that increase the vitality of the body to resist the spread of bacteria.

But although the principle is like this, it cannot be done like this in practice; if a large amount is rashly injected into the human body, it is true that the lesion may collapse, but severe systemic reactions will also occur; what happens in this regard, such as high fever, headache, nausea, vomiting, etc., will inevitably damage the patient's body. It may even cause life-threatening dangers.

Then, how should we start in the treatment of this disease? It is based on the established practice of auto-immunization, applied to patients to achieve the purpose of treatment. The method starts with extremely small doses, and then slowly and gradually increases to large doses. This method allows the patient to gradually become accustomed to the medicinal power; as the dose gradually increases, the medicinal power becomes greater, and the patient's resistance also becomes greater, and the body's organs also become stronger day by day; the power to resist the spread of tubercle bacillus toxin will naturally increase accordingly. If the patient has good adaptability, this dose can eventually be increased to half a cubic centimeter or one cubic centimeter. But the initial dose is only about one hundred thousandth, which shows the huge difference in dosage before and after! Therefore, patients who receive this treatment need a very long period. Generally, the period required for each dose is at least three months, usually about six months, or even up to a year. If it is less than three months, it has no value in treatment. The use of tuberculin is usually best done by subcutaneous injection; generally, two injections per week, and only one injection when using large doses. If a reaction occurs, the dose for the next injection must not be increased, at most limited to maintain the injection dose of the previous injection. In addition to the subcutaneous injection procedure, there are also intradermal injection procedures, and there are also two methods of intradermal inoculation and rubbing; but none of them are as common as subcutaneous injection, and doctors use them less in clinical practice, so they are all omitted here!

Talking Points

Starting with the Story of a Peddler Cutting His Thigh to Treat His Parent 224

— Meng Ruo

In the local newspaper on the 7th, I saw the following piece of news: Liu Hongxin, a native of Yangzhou, 22 years old, is a peddler of rattan boxes, living in Yinghua Lane. Hongxin has a mother, Huang, 48 years old, who has always had stomach pain, which comes and goes. This time, Huang's old illness recurred and suddenly became serious. She was bedridden and moaning. Liu Hongxin had read a small book and knew that there was such a thing as cutting one's thigh to treat one's parent. At 11 o'clock the night before, he carried a sharp knife and went secretly to an open space on Xiaoshadu Road. He cut a piece of meat from his left arm, about two inches long. At that time, a Western policeman was patrolling and saw him holding a sharp knife. His behavior was suspicious and he was taken to the police station. Later, Liu Hongxin explained the situation of cutting his thigh to treat his parent. Seeing that his left arm was injured, he was sent to the hospital for bandaging. The injury was not serious.

Liu Hongxin is indeed a filial son. He saw that his mother's old illness had recurred and suddenly became serious. In order to treat her, he did not hesitate to cut a piece of meat from his left arm with a sharp knife. This is not easy for ordinary people to do. But although Liu Hongxin's filial piety is commendable, he is still a foolish filial son, who does not understand that if his mother is sick, she should see a doctor for treatment. It cannot be cured by a piece of meat. However, the reason why he cut the meat was not a method that he came up with out of thin air. He wanted to use meat instead of medicine, saying that he was trying to treat his mother's stomach pain. But he learned it from a book. It turned out that he usually reads small books and knows that the ancients had the story of "cutting one's thigh to treat one's parent". Therefore, he was driven by filial piety and learned to be a filial son. He didn't know that the result was not only that he cut the meat and hurt himself, but it also did not help his mother's illness in the slightest. Moreover, because he was holding a sharp knife and his behavior was suspicious, he was taken to the police station by the Western policeman for questioning. Liu Hongxin can be said to be "his filial piety is commendable, and his foolishness is beyond compare".

However, what we want to say here is not to praise Liu Hongxin and give him the beautiful name of "filial son" to promote benevolence and save the decadent customs. What we should pay attention to is the great influence of words. In the past, we heard that three apprentices, after reading novels such as "The Strange Heroes of the Jianghu", suddenly became obsessed and went to the mountains together to find Taoism and seek immortality, imitating the stories of the strange heroes. There was also Shi Jianqiao, who assassinated Sun Chuanfang not long ago. This filial daughter avenged her father. According to her own confession, it was because she read the story of "Shang Sanguan" in Liaozhai, which was deeply imprinted in her mind. She thought that although the story was fabricated, the fact was not impossible. Therefore, she decided to assassinate and do something that shocked society. The sentence "I dare not forget my father's hatred for a moment" in the leaflet she distributed was also copied from the original sentence in the "Yu Jiang" chapter of Liaozhai. From these facts, we can see the depth of the influence of words. A "Strange Heroes of the Jianghu" can call three apprentices to go to the mountains to find Taoism and seek immortality. A section of "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio" can make a woman avenge her father. A story of "cutting one's thigh to treat one's parent" can induce a peddler to cut a piece of meat to treat his mother's illness. The influence of words is so amazing.

How should people engaged in education and culture pay attention to this point? Although our country has been baptized by foreign new ideas in recent times, the feudal consciousness in society is still very common. We must eliminate this old force in the future, starting from the cultural aspect, so that everyone can establish a correct consciousness that is in line with modern life. The authorities should conduct an inspection of the cultural circles in our country, and eliminate everything that is not suitable for today. In this way, all unreasonable behaviors in society may be expected to gradually decrease. We feel very dangerous when we see the prevalence of many bad books on the market.

Scenic Line of Desolate Borders 225

— Hei Ding

Winter.

The cold wind whipped through Balamacun, home to the Daur people near the lower reaches of the Girin River, already creating a deathly, indifferent scene. The boundless wilderness was covered with a thick layer of white snow. The Girin River, like a wide, white ribbon, meandered and lay still on the left side of Gahashan Mountain.

It was just after lunchtime. The five-year-old (implied: older than 50) Lu Zhisuo, shivering, and his ten-year-old grandson, Biya, were urging their dog sled back along the mountain path of Cikun Mountain. Biya's small face was red and flushed, as if he had drunk a few cups of wine. He wore a large, shaggy dog-skin hat on his head. His eyes were so covered that he could barely see the road ahead. As he walked, he kept pushing the hat up on his head with his hand, which was hidden in a leather glove. He also puffed out his cheeks, wrinkled his nose, and muttered:

— Damn your mother...

The hat was pushed almost to the point of falling off.

Lu Zhisuo took out a dry tobacco pipe from a leather bag on his back, packed it with tobacco, struck a match with a "scratch" sound, and started puffing on it. He heard Biya muttering and opened his dry lips to grumble:

— I told you not to wear it this morning, but you wouldn't listen. Didn't your mother tell you, but you wouldn't listen. If you do that again, you won't come out with me. If you hadn't come today, would that old fox have escaped? It's all your fault, all your fault...

Biya became unhappy with his grandfather's grumbling, and his face was covered with anger. He stubbornly walked ahead of his grandfather, head down, not paying attention to anything.

Dozens of steps away from the village, three elderly men stood by the river, chatting loudly. Among the three men were Lu Zhisuo's neighbor, Baske, and two others who came from elsewhere. As soon as Baske saw Lu Zhisuo coming from the mountain path, he raised his hand, raised his voice, and shouted:

— Hey, Old Lu, are you lucky? You must have caught a lot again?

The sound reached Lu Zhisuo's ears, causing him to suddenly lift his face and take a look. Then, he waved his palm, showing a very frustrated look, and replied as he walked:

— Lucky? If I was any luckier, I wouldn't be able to pull the dog sled back!

He coughed, paused, and continued:

— It's all because of this kid, Biya. If he hadn't come, I wouldn't have let that old fox escape! Hmph, lucky? Look, the dog sled is coming back empty.

— This is really, this is really...

Baske sighed repeatedly.

Lu Zhisuo had already approached Baske. He stopped and smiled at the two elderly men standing next to Baske on his left. Then, he asked Baske:

— These two?

He also smiled knowingly at the two elderly men.

At that moment, Baske was reaching out to grasp Biya's wrist, opening his mouth, which reeked of alcohol from having just drunk, and drunkenly said:

— Hey, to be able to go hunting in the mountains with your grandfather at the age of ten is really a capable little fellow.

He kept laughing.

Baske heard Lu Zhisuo asking him, quickly turned his face, and with a calm attitude and urgent tone, introduced the two elderly men to Lu Zhisuo:

— This is Bitun Ku, and this is Chaisi Tai. They are from Gesaer Town.

Lu Zhisuo nodded, put on an enthusiastic look, and kindly asked the two elderly men:

— Oh, oh, such a long way, you two must be here for something, right?

Before they could speak, Baske quickly interjected:

— Don't you know? Gesaer Town has also been occupied by ×

Page 18

× soldiers! It was just occupied yesterday. These two escaped from the town!

Lu Laisuo shuddered. He stared blankly, speechless. After a long time, he slowly said in his throat:

— Oh, escaped...

Seemingly thinking, he sighed with some anger:

— Alas, the world has changed! This is a great disaster! How did ×× soldiers occupy that place, and now they are coming to seize this place...

The atmosphere could no longer be calm. Then, Bitun Ku, who had just been introduced by Baske, unconsciously clenched his fist, widened his eyes, and said bitterly:

— The town was in chaos yesterday! ×× soldiers came from Girin, more than two hundred of them! As soon as they arrived in the town, they searched every household one by one. And they confiscated all the firearms in the town. There's also a rumor that in a few days, they will even confiscate the homemade guns that we hunters use.

Lu Zhisuo was so frightened that he gasped for air, and said:

— What, what, even the homemade guns that we hunters use...?

Bitun Ku took out a dry tobacco pipe from his robe, smoked it, and said:

— This is really hopeless. What else can we rely on for a living! Alas! Alas... I heard that the Gularin area has also been very chaotic recently, with many more ×× soldiers. They all say that they are preparing to fight the Big Nose Country (Note 1), but I don't know if it's true or false... Now disaster has come upon us! Everyone in the town has fled today. Because this morning, two ×× soldiers died on the street, covered in blood. It looked like they were killed last night...

Before Bitun Ku could finish, Chaisi Tai, who had been silent for a long time, anxiously interrupted:

— Today, the town was like the sky had fallen. ×× soldiers arrested a lot of people, some Solun people, some Oron people, and some Biral people. They killed them all without asking questions. ×× soldiers also said that we were going to rebel, but they are the ones rebelling! They won't let us live...

— Nuoya, Nuoya... (Note 3)

A few sighs from women could be heard in the distance. Then, the voices of women calling their children could be heard.

At this time, the large group of children playing, pulling sleds, and ice skating on the riverside at both ends of the town, suddenly heard this wildfire-like shocking news, and everyone was so frightened that their faces changed. They stood still, as if they had lost their souls. Some of them shouted hoarsely:

— Oh my! ×× soldiers are coming! Where can we run?

The children all ran home.

Biya also urged the dog sled and ran home.

Lu Zhisuo's pale face was covered with a gloomy, depressed color. After a long time, he seemed to wake up from a nightmare and muttered in a hoarse voice:

— Then, then, what are we going to do? If our hunting guns are really confiscated, will we have any way to survive...?

His voice trembled. After a while, he said again:

— Baske, do you think ×× soldiers can come to our place from Gesaer Town again?

Baske shook his head and said he didn't know. At the same time, Bitun Ku and Chaisi Tai said in unison:

— Who can guarantee that? They can occupy wherever they want. Who can stop them...?

Suddenly, a mournful cry was blown by a gust of wind from afar:

— Years of rebellion! Nuoya! Nuoya!

This was Lu Zhisuo's old wife, Yishaya, who had rushed from home to the street, muttering and sighing. She was still a distance away from Lu Zhisuo when she hurriedly asked loudly:

— Is it true? The ×× soldiers have occupied Gesaer Town?

Lu Zhisuo pretended not to hear and didn't bother to answer her, just worrying himself.

Yishaya stopped.

Baske glanced at Yishaya, widened his eyes, and said:

— I'm afraid they will come to our place too...

Nuoya, Nuoya! What can we do? I'm going home to ask the Bodhisattva to bless us...

Yishaya muttered and limped home.

Lu Zhisuo silently followed behind his old wife Yishaya, walking, walking.

Dusk. Balamacun was deathly silent, and there was no one walking on the street.

Late at night. Balamacun was even more deathly silent, and a strong wind was blowing on the street.

Lu Zhisuo didn't sleep. He quietly knelt in front of the Bodhisattva, propped up his heavy, drowsy eyelids, his two melancholy eyes turning and turning, and said:

— Gaga! (Note 3) Bless Balamacun, bless us hunters...

Note: 1. They all call Russia the Big Nose Country.

2. Heavenly Grandfather, Heavenly Grandfather.

3. A term for God.

Sea 226

— Shi Weizhi

The sea is familiar to me.

I have seen it smile, under the warm sun, blowing a gentle breeze, the surface of the sea shimmering with golden water snakes, the water droplets jumping, like innocent children running and playing in the prairie; I have also seen its anger, the surface of the sea only hearing a roar, the waves rolling up higher than people, falling back to hit the stones on the shore, the sound can deafen people; I have also seen the sea's...

When the sea smiles, I am intoxicated, my heart is taken away by the jumping water droplets, I seem to fall in the great loving sea; when the sea is angry, I lower my head, I feel the insignificance of myself, before this great sea.

And also at this time, I can't help but shed tears. I am moved, I can only shed tears; besides shedding tears, what else can I do?

The sea is roaring again, still mixed with the bloody wind, my eyes feel another heat. With this resolution, I will be moved to tears again, but also with this resolution, besides shedding tears, I will also throw my insignificant self into the great sea, to shed a drop of blood, because I know that the great sea is originally made up of countless insignificant selves.

Film

"Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" and the Scenery of Qingdao 231

"Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" is a creation by the playwright Hong Shen, published in "Literature". The play is set in Qingdao and is a wonderful film based on historical facts. In the twenty-third year of Guangxu in the former Qing Dynasty, Germany used the excuse of a priest being killed to send warships to occupy Jiaozhou Bay and seize it as a "concession"; after decades of deliberate management, Qingdao became an important commercial port and a military stronghold.

The mountains surrounding Qingdao are all built with forts, and among the green grass and trees, there are hidden heavy artillery with a caliber of more than ten inches - and flat roads have been built along the mountains and coasts to provide access to all directions. As for the city, there is no place that is not a magnificent building, and the tall foreign houses show a very prosperous scene. After the Xinhai Revolution, the surviving Qing elders and officials of the fallen country liked the protection of foreign forces in this place and regarded it as "Peach Blossom Spring Today"; they moved their families and settled down, and all were prepared to spend their old age in this countryside. However, good times did not last long. In the autumn of the third year of the Republic of China, the European War broke out, and Qingdao was seized by the Japanese Empire. "Ghosts fighting ghosts", needless to say, the losers are the Chinese people in our semi-colonial state. As a result, the tragedy of some surviving Qing elders and officials of the fallen country occurred. "Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" also points out the problem of survival for the people of semi-colonial China in this turbulent era.

Dentsu Stage Play Fully Mobilized 232

Dentsu Company will stage Chekhov's three famous plays for the first time, directed by Sun Shiyi and Xu Xingzhi. Director Sun directed the two plays "The Boor" and "The Anniversary", and Director Xu directed "The Proposal". In order to emphasize the plot, the two directors have slightly modified the script to increase interest.

The actors are particularly suitable for the personalities of the characters in Chekhov's three famous plays staged by Dentsu this time: the amorous Wang Ying plays the widow in "The Boor"; the vicious Jin Shan plays the debt collector in the play; as for the girl in "The Proposal", she is played by the petite Miss Chen Bo'er; the smiling Shi Chao plays a neighbor; the father is played by the old-fashioned Tian Lie, and the cast in "The Anniversary" are also very appropriate. The hot-handed and foot-handed Lan Ping plays the old woman; the extremely bored Gu Er plays the bookkeeper; the showy Lu Luming plays the chairman's wife; and the outwardly strong and inwardly weak cartoonist Cai Ruohong plays the chairman. The actors sat around the stove and rehearsed their lines, and although it was the cold winter season, it felt as warm as spring.

All the costumes for Dentsu's premiere are designed by Xu Xingzhi, with Lan Ping as a consultant, to ensure beauty and suitability. They are being rushed to production immediately.

In terms of stage design, Zhang Yunqiao, an expert in stage design, has been hired to draw three full-color stage drawings, which will be distributed to carpenters to build according to the drawings.
